   Bytes  Format Units Label  Explanation
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   1-  4  I4     ---     ID        Source identification number
   6- 10  F5.2   kpc     DIST      Adopted distance
  12- 16  F5.2   kpc   e_DIST      Uncertainty in VLSR
  18- 22  F5.2   kpc     DIST_C	   Distance from Elia et al. (2021)
  24- 29  F6.2   kpc     DIST_M    Distance from Mege et al. (2021)
  31- 36  F6.2   kpc   e_DIST_M    Uncertainty in distance from Mege et al. (2021)

  55- 59  F5.2   kpc     DIST_R1   Most probable RDF distance
  61- 65  F5.2   kpc   e_DIST_R1   Uncertainty in most probable RDF distance
  67- 70  F4.2   ---     PINT_R1   Integrated probability for most probable RDF distance
  72- 76  A5     ---     ARM_R1    Name of associated spiral arm for most probable RDF distance (1)
  78- 82  F5.2   kpc     DIST_R2   Second-most probable RDF distance
  84- 87  F4.2   kpc   e_DIST_R2   Uncertainty in second-most probable RDF distance
  89- 92  F4.2   ---     PINT_R2   Integrated probability for second-most probable RDF distance

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
